Property movements suggest a return to Sokovian-region holdings; a renewed program of acquisitions in his library (now expanding into bioethics, AI governance, climate-systems literature — he is updating his doctrine for the next century); a near-cessation of public-facing crime.

This is the closest the subject comes, in the middle period, to *stillness.* The surveillance file should mark it as such, because it is genuinely rare. He is not at peace; he is in a long inhale.

---

## IX. The Born Better Excursion — The Bloodline Audit

Within this stiller interval the subject undertakes the bloodline-investigation arc — a methodical, almost forensic study of every prior Baron Zemo back to the medieval founder. He goes to the archives himself. He reads the parish records, the estate ledgers, the inquisitorial transcripts. He time-displaces, by available means, to verify in person where verification is possible. The findings are unambiguous: the Zemos have been, with statistical reliability across centuries, *monsters* — pillagers, torturers, collaborators, opportunists. The lineage he has organized his life around is morally indefensible at every node.

The diagnostic question is what he does with this information. He does not repudiate the name. He does not change it. He does not retire. He *redefines the mission* — concluding that his task is not to vindicate the lineage as it was but to be the Zemo who *redeems* it by imposing order rather than extracting from chaos. This is, structurally, the same move his life has always made: the only available frames are *better Zemo* or *worse Zemo,* never *not Zemo.* The Born Better arc is the formal proof of the limitation. He has audited the lineage and chosen to continue it; the audit was never a real exit.

The subsidiary admission inside the arc is, however, historically significant: it is the first time he allows himself, internally and aloud, to articulate that **Heinrich was wrong.** Not contemptible — not yet — but *wrong.* The reaction formation that the Citizen V identity dramatized in costume is finally said in words. The middle period closes with that sentence half-spoken.

---

## X. Pattern Consolidation Across the Middle Period

Pulling back from the individual arcs, the longitudinal signal of the middle period is the *stabilization of the operating system*:

1. **Plan-symbol-cruelty-collapse cycle.** The same four-beat escalator appears in every major engagement: clean strategic plan, symbolic flourish inserted for the subject's own satisfaction, personal-cruelty escalation against a Cap-adjacent target, catastrophic tactical error. The cycle is fully formed by the Mansion sequence and recurs through Liberators-era engagements with only superficial variation. He does not interrupt it. He may not be able to.

2. **Cover-identity virtuosity.** The Thunderbolts proves that he can simulate any role indefinitely at the behavioral level. The recurring failure is at the *motivational* level — he cannot model the desire to be what he is pretending to be, and so cannot predict that desire in others. This becomes, after the Thunderbolts, a permanent blind spot he is aware of and still cannot correct.

3. **Doctrine as the metabolizer of grievance.** Across the middle period, the personal wound is progressively converted into a political program. The conversion is real — by the Liberators arcs the doctrine is sufficient to direct operations on its own, without Cap as a target — but it is also incomplete: Rogers re-entry reliably collapses the doctrinal mode back into vendetta mode within a short interval. The doctrine is dominant in Cap's absence; the wound is dominant in Cap's presence. The subject lives in alternation between them.

4. **Recruitment grammar.** Two-axis selection (capability × exploitability) in the Masters of Evil and early Thunderbolts; one-axis selection (ideological compatibility) by the Liberators era. The shift is a learned response to the Thunderbolts collapse. He is one of the few villains in his weight class who *updates his recruitment heuristics* across engagements.

5. **Hood discipline.** Across the middle period the cowl moves from being a wound-covering necessity to being a *brand and ritual.* He dons it deliberately, in private, before engagements. It is the gesture by which he becomes the operative self. By the end of the middle period the hood is no longer about the face beneath; it is about the man it makes him into when he puts it on.

6. **Honor in the narrow sense.** Across every engagement of the middle period he keeps the letter of negotiated agreements with peer adversaries. He lies to publics, manipulates subordinates, betrays states — but a deal struck face-to-face with a recognized peer is, by his lights, sacred. This is not virtue; it is aristocratic self-image. It is also, operationally, the basis on which any future negotiation with him can be conducted.

7. **The Rogers-shaped hole.** Across every arc of the middle period, the most stable predictor of the subject's tactical performance is the proximity of Captain America. Distance correlates with competence; proximity correlates with self-defeat. The middle period does not produce any reduction in this coefficient. Whatever else he has learned, he has not learned this.

---

The middle period is, in summary, the interval in which the subject becomes fully himself: a first-rate strategic intellect operating an aristocratic political doctrine on a substrate of un


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# CHRONOLOGY IV — RECENT HISTORY & CURRENT STATE

## Subject: Helmut Julius Fritz Zemo, 13th Baron Zemo

---

## IV.1 — Framing the Window

The "recent" window for this subject is best dated from his deliberate withdrawal from open superhuman geopolitics following the dissolution of his last legitimate command structure, through the period of incarceration in the high-security facility, through his post-incarceration drift, and into the present operational posture: a man who has chosen to no longer wear a uniformed army around himself, and instead operates through favors, networks, leverage, and the residual gravitational pull of his name. The behavioral content of this era is **consolidation under reduced visibility** — a contraction of operational surface area combined with a deepening of the ideological program. The subject is, in the simplest formulation, *quieter and more dangerous than at any prior point in his life.*

---

## IV.2 — The Pre-Incarceration Collapse

The terminal phase of the subject's last open-field operation followed the pattern established across every prior cycle: a strategically elegant infrastructure project (this iteration centered on the controlled exposure of a population to compounds derived from his father's research, framed publicly as crisis-response) collapsed not because the architecture failed but because the subject, within reach of completion, elected the symbolic flourish over the closing move. He was, again, in proximity to a Rogers-adjacent figure and a Barnes-adjacent figure at the moment of breakdown. The escalation ladder ran true to template: strategic play → symbolic flourish → personal cruelty → tactical error. He was taken alive, which is itself diagnostic — he had structured the endgame so that capture remained an option. He does not want to die in a way his father did. The capture is a chosen survival.

He surrendered without significant violence, dressed correctly, and asked the arresting officer (in the officer's own language) whether the man's family had emigrated from a particular village in Saxony. The officer's family had. The subject knew this. The detail is the man.

---

## IV.3 — The Incarceration Phase

### IV.3.a — Facility and conditions

He was housed in a maximum-security detention environment designed for individuals of high cognitive endowment and high social-engineering capacity — concrete, glass, single-occupancy, restricted contact, surveillance density approaching one camera per twenty cubic meters of cell volume. The subject's cell during this period contained: a bunk, a fixed writing surface, a small shelf of permitted reading material (he requested and was granted works in four languages — confirmed titles include a German-language edition of Clausewitz, a French *Mémoires d'outre-tombe*, an English-language compilation of Thucydides, and a Russian volume of Akhmatova, the last unexpected and unexplained), no personal effects beyond regulation, and — notably — no mask. The mask was confiscated. He did not request its return. **He does not need the mask in a room he has accepted as his.**

### IV.3.b — Behavior in custody

The subject was a *model prisoner* in the manner of a man who has decided that compliance is the most aggressive available posture. He woke at the same hour every day (estimated 05:40 local), performed a calisthenic régime of approximately forty minutes (recorded: variations on the Tibetan rite sequence, isometric holds, no equipment), bathed, dressed in regulation attire with the collar adjusted half a centimeter higher than issued, ate without complaint, and read for the permitted hours. He spoke to guards in their first languages where possible. He learned the names of their children. He never asked for anything.

His engagements with institutional psychiatry during this phase were of a piece with prior canon: he studied his evaluators. One evaluator — a woman of senior credentials — abandoned the assessment after the fourth session, citing a vague clinical reason; the actual reason, reconstructable from session notes, was that the subject had begun to comment, gently and without malice, on aspects of her personal life he could not have learned through any channel she had authorized. He had reconstructed her from the cadence of her questions, the wear pattern on her wedding band, and a brand of pen she used in the second session and not the third. He apologized when asked to stop. He did not stop.

### IV.3.c — The reading-room economy

Within six months he had established a functional information economy with three other inmates and at least two guards. Currency was favors of attention: he listened to a man describe his daughter's wedding for nine consecutive visits and the man eventually walked a folded note out of the wing for him. The note's content is not in the file. The relationship is.

This is the period to be most carefully understood: **he is not idle in custody. He is networking at slow speed.** Every conversation is a deposit. He will collect over years.

### IV.3.d — Extraction

His departure from the facility was not, properly speaking, an escape — escape is a category that implies violence against the institution. It was an *extraction*, transactional, accomplished through the activation of a relationship that had been instrumented during incarceration plus one external lever pulled by a party who needed his particular cognitive output for a specific window. He walked out in borrowed clothes, was driven to a service road, and was on a different continent within thirty-six hours. The facility's after-action review identified six points of failure; the subject's hand is visible at four of them and arguably at all six.

He did not retaliate against any individual who had detained him. He sent, six weeks later, an unsigned arrangement of white lilies to the funeral of the senior guard who had been most decent to him during his stay. The guard had died of unrelated cardiac causes. The flowers were the message: *I remember decency. I remember everything.*

---

## IV.4 — The Withdrawal Period

### IV.4.a — Geography and tradecraft

The eighteen months following extraction are the most lightly documented in the file. He moved on a rotation through cities chosen for *cultural depth* over operational utility — Vienna, Trieste, Tbilisi, Lisbon, a coastal segment of Croatia, two weeks in Istanbul, a quiet period in Quebec City that no one had predicted. He travels light. He travels often. He travels well. His documents are excellent; he does not produce them himself, but he selects his forger the way other men select a tailor and pays accordingly.

Lodging during this period favored: small residential hotels run by families into the second or third generation; rented apartments arranged through intermediaries who never met him in person; once, a borrowed country house belonging to a man who owed the Zemo family a debt three generations old and was startled but unsurprised to be called upon. He does not stay anywhere long enough to develop a barista. He **deliberately denies himself rituals of place** because rituals leave residue.

### IV.4.b — Daily structure (reconstructed)

Wake before dawn. The forty-minute calisthenic régime. Coffee — black, single cup, never a refill. A walk of between forty-five and seventy minutes, route varying but always involving at least one bridge or open square (he prefers sightlines and reads exits). Reading from approximately 09:00 to 12:00 — current, periodicals, history, biography, occasionally fiction (he reads novels for the social information). A small lunch, usually cold. Correspondence in the afternoon — handwritten, posted from drop boxes that are not his nearest, mailed in batches that mix three or four addresses to thin the pattern analysis. A second walk in the late afternoon. Dinner at a restaurant rather than at home roughly four nights a week — he sits where he can see the door, tips correctly without overtipping, leaves no signature dish or wine. He reads after dinner for one to two hours, then sleeps. He has slept approximately six and a quarter hours per night for as long as records exist on him. He does not vary this.

The régime is monastic. It is also a tell — a man who lives this regularly is conserving cognition for *one project of consuming scale.*

### IV.4.c — Wardrobe and presentation

Without the cowl, he presents in the manner of an academic of independent means: well-cut but unshowy wool, dark colors, the collar always slightly higher than the prevailing fashion, gloves more often than is strictly seasonal. He travels with a single hard-sided case and a softer leather bag containing the sword (disassembled, the blade as a separate carry under the appropriate documentation as a sport-épée; he is correctly licensed in every jurisdiction in which he carries it — *he files the paperwork*). The mask travels in the hard case, wrapped in unbleached linen. He has not been seen wearing it in public during this period. He puts it on, observers report on the few occasions a sighting has been confirmed, only when **he is preparing to act in his own name.** It has become a vestment.

### IV.4.d — Affect

He is calmer than at any prior point in the longitudinal record. The Ellis-era philosophical austerity has deepened into something approaching equanimity. He smiles more — small, dry, correctly timed. He laughs once or twice a week, briefly, at things that are genuinely funny. His French has acquired a slight Belgian lilt that was not there a decade ago, suggesting prolonged contact with at least one Belgian interlocutor whose identity is not in the file. He drinks slightly more than he used to — still controlled, still ceremonial, but the second glass appears now where there used to be only the first. This is not decay. It is permission. **He has begun to allow himself small pleasures because he has decided he has earned them.**

---

## IV.5 — Current Operational Posture

### IV.5.a — No standing army

The most striking feature of the present configuration is what is *absent*. He commands no team. He has not attempted to assemble Masters of Evil, Thunderbolts, Liberators, or any analog in the current window. The Born Better insight — that the lineage produces monsters and the corrective is order rather than conquest — has matured into a working method: he no longer wants to be *seen* leading. He wants outcomes; he is indifferent to credit; he has, finally, internalized that credit is a *cost.*

### IV.5.b — Operational modality

The present mode is **leverage at distance.** He maintains a dispersed network of approximately (estimated) forty to sixty individuals across roughly a dozen jurisdictions who owe him favors, fear him, share fragments of his worldview, or are managed by combinations of the three. He activates them sparingly. He has not, in the present window, asked any single contact for more than one significant favor — he is *amortizing* the network rather than spending it. The contrast with the Masters-of-Evil era is total: where he once stood at the center of a visible pyramid of force, he now sits at the center of an invisible mesh of obligation.

The favors requested and granted in the present window cluster around: information access (financial flows, security architecture diagrams, biographical detail on specific targets), document quality, transportation through soft borders, the placement and removal of small items in specific locations. He has not, in the present window, ordered a killing through this network. This is **not** evidence of moral evolution; it is evidence that he has not yet judged a killing operationally necessary. The capacity is intact.

### IV.5.c — The Barnes/Rogers vector

The Cap fixation has not abated; it has *refined*. Rogers's contemporary status (variable across the canon, but the recent period finds him in some condition of altered presence — out of the suit, restored, replaced, or returned, depending on the arc state) is tracked by the subject with the meticulousness of a man maintaining a single, durable file. He receives, through one of his contacts, periodic open-source updates on Rogers's whereabouts and condition. He does not act on them. The file is maintained for the day on which action becomes appropriate. **He is willing to wait years for the correct moment.** He has waited decades before.

Barnes occupies an adjacent file, treated with a different texture. The subject's relationship to Barnes is, complicatedly, **closer to identification than to hatred** — Barnes is also a man who became what was done to him, also a man fused to a legacy he did not choose, also a man with conditioning underneath his face. The subject has not, in the present window, attempted to re-weaponize the trigger conditioning. The restraint is calculated: the trigger words are, in his hands, a one-shot weapon, and he is preserving the round.

### IV.5.d — The ideological project

The present iteration of the long-standing autocratic ideology has taken on a more *curatorial* tone. He no longer speaks (in the few recorded utterances captured by intercept during this window) of *conquering* anything. He speaks of *pruning.* The framing has shifted from gardener to surgeon. The targets he discusses in private conversation are: specific institutions he regards as catastrophically corrupt, specific superhuman individuals he regards as net negatives to global order, specific concentrations of power he regards as misallocated. He is, in his own self-understanding, performing **selective subtraction from the world** in service of order. This is the most coherent and the most dangerous he has ever been ideologically, precisely because the program has been pared down to actions a small number of people could plausibly accomplish.

### IV.5.e — Financial state

The Zemo holdings — drawn down across decades of operations and family disgrace — are smaller than they once were and larger than they appear. He maintains liquidity in at least four currencies through instruments held by intermediaries; he has access to a small number of high-value physical assets (art, primarily — two confirmed pieces of pre-war German expressionism, one Dutch still life that should be in a museum, a Persian carpet of significant provenance kept in storage in Geneva). He does not live richly. He lives *correctly* for a man of his station, which is a different thing. The aristocratic affect requires less money than people assume; it requires *taste*, which is free, and *patience*, which compounds.

---

## IV.6 — Current State: Somatic and Cognitive

### IV.6.a — Body

Late middle age, maintained at peak human conditioning through the régime described above. Resting heart rate (estimated from observable indicators) in the low fifties. Posture is upright and economical; gait is unhurried but covers ground efficiently — he does not walk fast, but he is never late. Sword arm shows no degradation; he still spars (privately, on a circuit of perhaps three trusted partners across Europe, one of whom is a retired Olympic-level fencer who does not know his student's name). Hands are scarred along the dorsal surfaces — old work — but uncalloused in a way that suggests gloves more than soft living. The face beneath the hood remains as canonically described: melted, fused, the topography of a wound that was deliberate. He shaves it. He maintains it. It is **his**, and he has stopped flinching from his own mirror.

### IV.6.b — Mind

Eidetic recall intact and arguably sharper — he has spent decades training the instrument and it has not yet begun to dull. Linguistic capacity expanding rather than contracting (he has acquired functional Turkish in the present window, working on Mandarin). Reading appetite undiminished. Strategic horizon has *lengthened* — current planning operates on timelines of five to fifteen years, and he discusses these timelines in the unconcerned manner of a man who fully expects to be present for the payoff. He is not afraid of dying. He is afraid of dying *before the work is finished*, which is a different and more useful fear.

### IV.6.c — Affect

The previously catalogued **strategic-IQ collapse in Cap's presence** remains, almost certainly, the unaddressed structural flaw. He has not been in Cap's presence in the present window. He has therefore not been tested. The reasonable inference is that the flaw is intact and that any face-to-face encounter with Rogers (or with a sufficiently Rogers-coded substitute) will produce the same cascade it has produced every other time. He has not interrupted the pattern; he has *avoided the trigger*, which is a sophisticated form of management but not a resolution.

---

## IV.7 — Where He Is Now

At the moment this section is compiled, the subject is, on best estimate, in a Central European city of medium size, in rented accommodation arranged through a third party, reading in the mornings and walking in the afternoons, eating dinner at a restaurant whose owner he addresses by patronymic, drafting correspondence in a hand so disciplined it could be mistaken for a typeface, occasionally receiving a visitor who stays for one drink and leaves with an instruction. The mask is in a linen wrap in a hard case in the wardrobe. The sword is in the corner. The file on Rogers is updated weekly. The file on Barnes is updated monthly. The ledger of favors owed is in his head, where no one can subpoena it.

He is, by every observable index, *content.* This is the single most concerning datum in the present section. A Helmut Zemo in physical comfort, in cognitive prime, in operational quiet, with a refined ideological program and a global network of obligations, who has stopped seeking adulation and started seeking outcomes, who has buried his sadism without renouncing it, who has accepted his face and kept the hood as a *uniform of office* rather than a bandage — this configuration of the subject has never previously existed in the longitudinal record.

He is also, by the structural logic of his pathology, **one provocation away from the same collapse he has executed every prior cycle.** The provocation will, eventually, come — Rogers will return to the field, or a Rogers-substitute will rise into the same iconic position, or the Citizen V legacy will be invoked in a public forum, or someone will speak Heinrich's name in the wrong tone in a room he is in. The cascade will run. He will choose the symbolic flourish over the closing move. He will lose, again, in the way he has always lost.

The interval before that provocation is the present interval. It is the most operationally productive period of his life. The file should be read accordingly: **he is using the quiet.**

— END CHRONOLOGY IV —


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: HELMUT JULIUS FRITZ ZEMO

*UATU Dossier, Section 4 of 11. Compiled from observed canon, reconstructed clinical inference, and the granular somatic record a total-surveillance file would preserve. The subject has never knowingly submitted to a complete physical examination by anyone he did not employ; what follows is therefore assembled from combat footage, custodial intake records during his several incarcerations, after-action reports from agents who fought him in close quarters, and the negative space of his own conspicuous concealments.*

---

## 1. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE AND DEVELOPMENTAL HEALTH

**Birth and infancy.** Delivered on the family estate by a private physician of the Zemo household rather than in a hospital — consistent with the elder Baron's pathological aversion to outside record-keeping and with the aristocratic preference for keeping the bloodline's medical data off civil rolls. There is, accordingly, no public birth-weight or APGAR record; the existing intake forms (the German pediatric file later seized during a sealed Interpol cooperation request, summarized in fragments across the V-Battalion's archive) describe a full-term male of unremarkable presentation, normal milestones, early advanced verbal acquisition.

**Childhood illnesses.** Standard European pediatric exposures: measles (pre-vaccination protocol in the household; the elder Baron preferred natural exposure), a documented bout of scarlet fever at approximately age six requiring two weeks of bed rest, and a recurring sinusitis through adolescence that produces, even now, the faint nasal quality detectable in his lower register when he is fatigued. No surgical interventions in childhood. No fractures. The estate's stable accidents — riding from age four, falls from age five — produced bruises and one mild concussion (age nine, observed by the steward, no medical workup) but nothing that left structural sequelae.

**Endocrine and growth.** Tall but not extraordinary (subject reads as a controlled, compact aristocrat rather than an imposing one); normal pubertal timing per estate physician's notes; no documented endocrine pathology. The musculature he carries into adulthood is built, not given.

**Dental.** Exceptional. Old-European dentistry of the conservative school — preservation over replacement — performed across his life by a single Zurich practitioner the family has retained for three generations. No crowns, no implants visible on the rare occasions his lower face has been imaged through the cowl. He has been observed to grind his back molars under stress, particularly during interrogations; mild bruxism, untreated, would be the expected finding.

**Vision and hearing.** Both intact at near-optimal levels into late middle age. The cowl's eye apertures are deliberately small; he has trained for decades in the resulting restricted visual field and his head-tracking compensates for it with a characteristic micro-rotation every two to three seconds when scanning. Hearing is unimpaired and reportedly acute — he has corrected subordinates on regional accents through a closed door.

---

## 2. THE CENTRAL EVENT — ADHESIVE X IMMERSION

The defining medical incident of the subject's life and the one toward which every subsequent somatic fact orients itself.

**Mechanism.** During the confrontation with Captain America that ended his Phoenix-alias debut, the subject fell into a vat of Adhesive X — the polymer compound his father had weaponized and that had previously fused Heinrich Zemo's hood permanently to his face. The compound is not a simple adhesive; the canonical descriptions and reverse-engineered formulations indicate a cross-linking polymer with strong covalent affinity for keratin and proteinaceous substrates, exothermic on contact with skin moisture, and capable of penetrating the epidermis to the level of the dermal-epidermal junction before completing its cure.

**Acute injuries sustained.** Full-face and partial-scalp chemical-thermal burn of mixed depth: superficial to partial-thickness across the lower face, with patches of full-thickness involvement along the cheekbones, jawline, and the bridge of the nose where the immersion was deepest. Inhalation injury to the upper airway (he was conscious and breathing when he went in); presumed brief corneal exposure — survived only because reflexive closure occurred in the half-second before submersion. The compound's cure-cycle locked tissue into a fixed topography before normal inflammatory swelling could redistribute it, which produced the signature feature of the disfigurement: not the smooth, contracted scarring of a healed burn but a frozen, sculptural distortion, as though the face had been caught mid-melt and arrested.

**Acute medical management.** None for the first critical hours — the subject extracted himself, fled, and reached private resources before any hospital became involved. The reconstructive work that followed was performed by black-market surgeons and, in later arcs, by physicians retained by the rebuilt Zemo holdings. The standard burn-care timeline (debridement, escharotomy, grafting) was either bypassed or performed badly; the topography that resulted is what one would expect from a severe chemical burn allowed to demarcate and contract without proper early intervention.

**Functional sequelae.**
- *Motor:* none of consequence. Facial musculature remains innervated and active. He can blink, speak, chew, swallow, and produce the full repertoire of micro-expressions; the subordinates who have heard him in private describe a face that "moves correctly under the wreckage."
- *Sensory:* patchy. Areas of full-thickness involvement are anesthetic; surrounding partial-thickness zones are hypersensitive, particularly to temperature change. He cannot tolerate cold wind on bare facial skin and reflexively turns his head from it on the rare occasions he is unmasked outdoors.
- *Thermoregulatory:* mildly impaired. Sweat-gland destruction across the involved areas reduces facial cooling; in heat or sustained exertion he loses heat through the scalp and neck disproportionately, which is one of several reasons the cowl's fabric weight and weave have evolved across his career.
- *Speech:* preserved. No labial or velar deficit. The slight nasal coloring of his speech is older than the burn (the childhood sinusitis); under the cowl, the fabric muffles the upper formants and produces the characteristic dry, contained timbre.
- *Mastication and swallowing:* preserved.
- *Olfactory:* reduced. Nasal mucosal injury from the inhalation component diminished his sense of smell by perhaps thirty to forty percent, on his own private estimate (overheard once, in a wine cellar, complaining of it as one complains of an old injury one has stopped expecting to recover from).

**Reconstructive attempts.** Multiple, across decades. A series of partial restorations performed in private clinics — grafting from thigh and back donor sites, dermabrasion, attempts at Z-plasty along the major contracture lines. Each produced a more presentable but never normal face; each was subsequently re-injured, re-eroded, or in one documented arc actively restored by exotic means (a Moonstone-class enhancement) and re-destroyed in a later confrontation. The clinical picture at the time of this dossier: a face that is intermittently more and less ruined depending on the most recent intervention, but stably and chronically *not normal*, with the patient himself having ceased to pursue cosmetic restoration as a goal. He no longer believes the face can be made whole and he no longer wishes it to be.

**Critical clinical-philosophical point.** The disfigurement is, by every measurable criterion, *not* functionally disabling. He can see, hear, breathe, eat, speak, and fight at peak human capacity. The mask is therefore not a prosthesis and not a medical appliance. **It is a chosen object, and its chosenness is the most important medical fact about him.** When asked (twice, on record, during incarcerations) why he wore it given full preserved function, the subject gave first a flippant answer about aesthetics and second — to a different examiner, years later — a quieter answer about not wishing to be looked at. The second is closer to the truth; the truth itself, which he has never spoken aloud, is that the cowl reproduces his father's mask-fusion as an act of devotional iconography, and to remove it permanently would be to admit Heinrich was a man and not a totem.

---

## 3. ORTHOPEDIC AND TRAUMATIC HISTORY

**High-altitude falls — three documented, several more inferred.**

The first major fall was from the Avengers Mansion roof during the climax of the Under Siege operation: estimated six stories onto sloped ornamental terrain. Survived — the published record leaves the survival itself unexplained, which in the surveillance frame implies either landing modification (he was observed to roll on contact) or an emergency intervention from a fleeing teammate not reported in primary sources. Sequelae consistent with the fall: probable hairline fractures of one or both calcanei (he favored his left heel for at least eight months thereafter in subsequent appearances, a slight stutter in his weight transfer detectable to a trained observer), a probable T11–L1 compression injury that did not require fixation but produced the modest reduction in lumbar extension visible in his fencing stance from that era forward, and an almost certain mild traumatic brain injury whose only legible sequela was a six-month period of uncharacteristically simplified planning before his cognitive ceiling returned.

The second major fall — from an aircraft during a Thunderbolts-era extraction, into water — was non-injurious; he had prepared for it.

The third — Liberators-era, from a collapsing energy-platform — produced a fractured left clavicle, evident in the subsequent arc by his right-handed-only sword work for several weeks and the slight protective hunch of the left shoulder he carried until the bone fully remodeled. Untreated by any modern physician; he set it himself or had a subordinate do so.

**Blade injuries.** A career fencer accumulates cuts. The subject's body bears the faint inventory of an old-school fencing master who has, additionally, used real blades in real combat: a thin pale linear scar across the right forearm extensor surface (a parry that arrived a quarter-second late, sometime in his twenties), a small puncture scar in the left lateral thigh (probably from a counter-attack in the 1990s — the canonical Thunderbolts material implies a duel against a turncoat operative), and, most diagnostically, **no cuts on the hands.** A man with no cuts on his hands at his level of blade-time is a man who has internalized hand-discipline so completely that his unconscious will sacrifice anything else first.

**Concussive history.** Multiple. He has been struck by Captain America — by the man, by the shield, and by objects propelled by both — on at least a dozen recorded occasions, and by other super-soldier-class combatants on others. He has shown remarkable cognitive resilience; the longitudinal record does *not* suggest CTE-pattern decline, in part because his trauma exposure is acute-episodic rather than the repetitive sub-concussive load that produces the syndrome. He does, however, display a single soft sign that would draw the attention of a careful neurologist: under sustained cognitive load late in an operation, a brief left-eyelid flutter, perhaps four to six beats, lasting under a second, never remarked upon, never (so far as the record shows) noticed by him.

**Knees, hips, lumbar spine.** The expected wear of a lifelong fencer and combatant. The subject's lunge is shorter than it was twenty years ago by perhaps three centimeters; his recovery from the lunge is fractionally slower. He has compensated by tightening his measure and increasing the geometric sophistication of his blade-work. There is, almost certainly, early bilateral knee osteoarthritis; he warms up for any physical engagement with a discreet sequence of ankle and knee rotations performed while seated, masked as adjustment of his boots.

**Hands.** Calloused along the index and middle metacarpals (sword grip); no Dupuytren's; mild ulnar deviation of the right fifth digit consistent with an old, badly-set boxer's fracture from his late teens (likely a striking injury in pre-villain training, never set by a physician). Fine-motor control is uncompromised.

---

## 4. INHALATIONAL, TOXICOLOGICAL, AND CHEMICAL EXPOSURES

The Zemo family's research portfolio, inherited and curated, means the subject has lived for sixty years inside a higher-than-baseline ambient exposure to exotic chemistries.

**Adhesive X — chronic, ongoing.** Trace residues persist in the cured polymer fused to his facial dermis; whether the substance continues to off-gas at clinically meaningful levels is unknown, but he has spent decades with the equivalent of an industrial polymer surface on his face, which cannot be without effect. Possible chronic mucosal irritation; possible endocrine-disrupting load; unknown long-term hepatic processing of slowly leached oligomers. He does not appear to care.

**Compound X / longevity agents.** The subject has had access to, and on documented occasions has self-administered, derivatives of his father's life-extension research. His usage pattern is the diagnostic finding: instrumental, episodic, and indifferent — he treats the compounds the way a soldier treats a field ration, not the way an addict treats a drug. There is no evidence of dependency, escalation, or compulsive self-administration. The pharmacological effect appears to be modest biological-age deceleration rather than reversal; he is, by chronology, older than he presents, but not implausibly so.

**Exotic battlefield exposures.** Across his career: gamma-tinged environments in proximity to certain teammates and adversaries; mutant-energetic discharges; the various unmeasurable chronal and dimensional exposures of the Born Better arc. None has produced a documented oncologic or hematologic consequence, which is itself remarkable and possibly explained by the longevity compounds' background effect on cellular repair.

**Recreational substances — alcohol.** Light, ceremonial, aristocratic. A single glass of a serious wine with dinner; brandy after operations; champagne at strategic inflection points (the ritual is not affectation — he genuinely uses small alcohol intake as a marker of completed phases). He has never been observed drunk. He guards cognitive clarity with the discipline of a man who regards his mind as his only true inheritance.

**Recreational substances — tobacco.** Occasional, almost exclusively cigars, almost exclusively after the close of an operational arc. The ritual rather than the chemistry.

**Recreational substances — anything else.** None. No recreational stimulant use, no opioid use (including for pain — the fall injuries above were managed, almost certainly, with willpower and ice). He regards intoxication as the surrender of the only faculty he respects in himself.

**Caffeine.** Heavy, sustained, ritualized: strong black coffee in the morning, espresso through operational periods, occasional tea (preferred: a Russian Caravan blend) in the evening. This is the only substance to which he has any plausible physiological dependency.

---

## 5. SOMATIC CONDITIONING AND MAINTENANCE

**Daily régime.** Reconstructed from incarceration cell-time logs, observation of training compounds, and the absence of the kind of decline a non-régimen would produce: ninety minutes of morning conditioning (calisthenic and isometric, low-equipment, prison-survivable), thirty to forty-five minutes of blade-work (solo drills, footwork, point-control exercises against suspended targets), twenty minutes of breath training (a controlled hypoventilation protocol he uses to extend underwater tolerance and to manage autonomic arousal in confrontation). Evening: stretching, joint mobility, and on most nights an additional thirty minutes of reading-while-walking, which he uses to integrate cognitive and physical activity.

**Sleep.** Short and disciplined. Five to six hours, consistent timing, near-immediate sleep onset (a trained skill). Light dream recall by his own report (rare; given in a single overheard remark to a subordinate). No documented parasomnias, though a careful observer of his incarceration footage will note a recurring period of REM-density activity in the early-morning hours during which his masked face turns sharply toward the cell door at intervals — content of dreaming is not directly inferable but the orientation is suggestive of vigilance dreams rather than processing dreams.

**Diet.** Spartan-aristocratic. Protein-forward, vegetable-heavy, low refined carbohydrate, generous fat. He eats slowly and finishes nothing he does not intend to finish — a habit traceable to early childhood discipline at the family table. He has been observed to refuse food offered by adversaries even when poisoning was operationally impossible; the refusal is identity, not caution.

**Body composition.** Sub-twelve-percent body fat, sustained into late middle age. Musculature of the lean wiry type favored by fencers — substantial in the legs, back, and shoulders, less developed in the chest, with the disproportionate forearm and wrist development characteristic of sword-trained lineages.

---

## 6. NEUROCOGNITIVE PROFILE

**Memory.** Eidetic or near-eidetic for visual and tactical material, demonstrated repeatedly across canon: reconstructing the full Masters of Evil roster from memory, reciting Avengers loadouts unprompted, recalling fortification details from sites he had visited once. Autobiographical memory presents with a peculiar selective vividness around the father, the death of the father, and every confrontation involving Captain America; the gaps are conspicuous in the inverse — the mother is not so much forgotten as systematically un-recalled.

**Attention.** Exceptional sustained attention; superior divided attention under stress (he has fought, planned, and conversed simultaneously on multiple recorded occasions). Vigilance does not decay across long operational windows the way it does in normal subjects; the cost, presumably, is the post-operational collapse documented obliquely by the contemplative withdrawals he takes between arcs.

**Executive function.** Elite, with the single replicable failure mode already documented elsewhere in this file: in proximity to Rogers, executive control narrows and is replaced by symbolic-ritual behavior. The pattern is so consistent it should be considered a clinical finding rather than a personality observation.

**Language.** Native German; English to native fluency with a controlled minimal accent he deploys or suppresses for effect; French to near-native; Russian to operational-fluent; reading knowledge of Latin and at least one Slavic language relevant to the family's Carpathian holdings; functional Italian. No language pathology of any kind.

---

## 7. PSYCHIATRIC CONTACT AND ENGAGEMENT WITH CLINICIANS

He has been formally evaluated, at minimum, during three incarcerations — by U.S. federal forensic psychiatry, by Norwegian custodial clinicians during a brief extradition pendency, and by an internal V-Battalion debriefer in one of the rare cooperative moments of the Citizen V dispute. The pattern across all three is the same and is itself diagnostically informative:

- He arrives early to sessions and sits before invited.
- He answers the first three or four questions with disarming candor on neutral material.
- He then begins, gently, to interview the interviewer.
- By the end of session two he knows more about the clinician than the clinician knows about him.
- He produces, on demand, exactly the affect the clinician is hoping to elicit, which renders the affect uninterpretable.
- He will discuss his father in abstract historical terms and refuse personal-affective material.
- He will not discuss his mother at all; asked, he changes the subject with a small smile and a precise non-sequitur.
- He produces an MMPI-style profile that is patently curated, which he expects the examiner to notice, which he uses to open a meta-conversation that further inverts the power dynamic.

He has never sought psychiatric care voluntarily. He has never requested medication. He has never participated honestly in a therapeutic relationship. The single fragment in the record that resembles an authentic disclosure occurred late in his Ellis-era custody arc, when an unobserved camera caught him, alone, removing the cowl in cell-shadow and sitting for nine minutes with his face uncovered before replacing it. He did not cry. He did not speak. He sat and breathed. That nine minutes is the closest the surveillance archive comes to the inner man.

---

## 8. THE MASK AS A MEDICAL OBJECT

The cowl deserves its own subsection because it is the single most consistent feature of the subject's somatic presentation and because, despite being non-prosthetic, it has had measurable physiological consequences over decades of continuous wear.

**Material and construction.** Heavy purple weave — over the years progressively upgraded toward a fabric with better breathability and thermal management, though the visual signature (vertical front seam, ragged lower hem) has been preserved with religious consistency. Lining: a moisture-wicking inner layer added in the modern era. The hood seats over the full head and neck and tucks beneath the high green collar of the tunic.

**Dermatologic consequences.** Chronic facial occlusion has produced, predictably, intermittent perioral and periorbital folliculitis; mild seborrheic colonization; the kind of low-grade dermatitis that any combatant who wears a balaclava develops. He manages it with a disciplined twice-daily cleansing routine using a single fixed product line he has used for thirty years, supplied through the same Zurich apothecary that handles his dental work.

**Respiratory consequences.** Slight rebreathing of warmed, humidified air, which he has habituated to so completely that he reports (overheard) that unmasked breathing feels "thin." This is partly proprioceptive adaptation and partly real — the cowl creates a microclimate at the face that has become his baseline.

**Thermoregulatory consequences.** Discussed above; net detriment in heat, slight benefit in cold.

**Postural consequences.** The cowl's weight is trivial but its visual-field restriction has produced, over decades, the characteristic compensatory head-and-shoulder carriage already noted — a small constant rotation of the head, a slightly elevated chin to maximize the lower visual aperture, a corresponding chronic mild tension in the suboccipital muscles. He stretches the suboccipitals nightly. He has never named the habit out loud.

**Psychological consequences (medical-adjacent).** Removal of the cowl produces measurable autonomic activation — elevated pulse, shallow breath, micro-tremor of the hands — *even in safe contexts.* He has trained against it but the response is not extinguishable. The mask is, in a real physiological sense, part of his homeostatic envelope; its removal is treated by his nervous system as exposure.

---

## 9. PROGNOSIS, RISK, AND THE THINGS THAT WILL EVENTUALLY KILL HIM

In the absence of a violent end — and the violent end is overwhelmingly probable — the subject would, on current trajectory, decline slowly across his seventh and eighth decades along the following lines: progressive bilateral knee osteoarthritis limiting his lunge; gradual lumbar stiffening; the slow erosion of the rapid-recovery margin that has allowed him to take and absorb the falls he has taken; mild age-related working-memory contraction that would not become functionally visible until very late given his enormous baseline reserve; a probable late hearing loss in the high frequencies from concussive exposures; almost certainly an eventual oncologic event in the facial or upper-airway tissues, given the chronic chemical insult, though the longevity compounds


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: HELMUT JULIUS FRITZ ZEMO

*Compiled from longitudinal observational composite; cross-indexed against captivity-period medical observation, infiltration footage from Avengers Mansion (1986), Thunderbolts-era public-appearance archive (1997–98), Raft and supermax intake telemetry, and field surveillance subsequent to the Born Better arc. The subject is masked in the great majority of recorded frames; the atlas below distinguishes (M) mask-on observations from (U) unmasked or partial-mask observations from (I) inferred-from-silhouette readings.*

---

## I. STANDING ARCHITECTURE — THE BASELINE BODY

The subject stands, when unobserved or believing himself unobserved, in a near-classical **fourth-position fencer's rest** rather than a military attention: weight 60/40 on the rear foot, the forward foot slightly outturned, knees unlocked, spine stacked from the sacrum up through a long cervical line that adds an apparent inch and a half to his actual height. When he believes himself observed, the weight redistributes to 50/50 and the shoulders drop a finger's width — a *conscious* relaxation that reads, paradoxically, as the most controlled posture in the room. He has trained out the aristocratic vice of looking aristocratic, and the result is that he looks more aristocratic than men who try.

Height holds at roughly 5'10"; functional reach is longer than the frame suggests because he keeps the **scapulae depressed and protracted-ready**, the carriage of a man who expects to draw a blade. The pelvis is neutral; there is no anterior tilt, no sway. The abdominal wall is held in light isometric tension at all waking moments — not braced, *engaged* — which has the second-order effect of regulating his breathing into a shallow diaphragmatic pattern even at rest.

**Hands at rest.** Left hand habitually rests at the hip where the sword-belt sits or would sit, thumb hooked, fingers loose. Right hand free, often at the small of his back when listening, or laid flat on a tabletop with fingers spread (a tell of attention, not relaxation — the spread fingers monitor surface vibration). He does not cross his arms. He has not crossed his arms on record in any captivity footage; the closure of the chest is something he reserves and does not give away.

**Foot placement under conversation.** Subject orients his lead foot to the **person he intends to kill next**, not the person he is addressing. This is an unconscious holdover from saber training and is, when correctly read, the single most actionable piece of behavioral intelligence in the file.

---

## II. GAIT AND LOCOMOTION

The walk is short-stride for his height — roughly 26 inches at cruising pace, where a man of his proportions would tend toward 30 — and the cadence is metronomic to within ±4% across surveillance segments of up to twenty minutes. He **does not vary tempo to match a companion**; the companion adjusts to him, which he registers without acknowledging.

The footfall is heel-then-ball, quiet, with a *brief* roll through the lateral edge that suggests long hours in fencing shoes. Stairs descended in a controlled drop, two-at-a-time only on operational tempo; ascended one-at-a-time with the trailing foot bringing-to (a parade-step echo from boyhood drilling). He does not look at his feet on uneven ground; he has mapped the surface in advance with peripheral vision two paces ahead.

**Turn pattern.** He pivots on the *rear* foot like a fencer addressing a new line, never on the lead. When changing direction in a corridor he describes a slight outside arc rather than cutting the corner, which keeps his blade-side away from the wall.

**Door behavior.** Enters rooms with the right hand free and the body angled at roughly 30° to the threshold — never square. Closes doors behind him with the heel or the back of the hand; the dominant hand stays uncommitted. Exits a room walking forward, not backing; he is not afraid of a turned back, which is itself a statement.

---

## III. THE HEAD, THE HOOD, AND THE FACE BENEATH

### The cowl as second skin (M)

The full-head purple cowl with its vertical front seam and ragged hem is donned with a precise four-step ritual: (1) cowl gathered at the crown with both hands, fingertips only — never the palm against the fabric exterior; (2) drawn down the occiput first, then forward over the brow, so the seam aligns by feel down the bridge of the nose; (3) the hem tugged twice at the nape, twice at the throat, by the *left* hand only; (4) a single half-second of stillness — eyes closed beneath the fabric — before he opens them and resumes motion. The ritual takes between 11 and 14 seconds and is invariant. Captivity footage confirms he performs an abbreviated version (steps 3 and 4 only) when the cowl has been disturbed by combat.

He does not adjust the cowl in public. Once seated, it is fixed. Micro-adjustments are made only behind cover — entering a vehicle, turning to a sideboard, rounding a corner.

The cowl is **breathed through** with a learned modification: a slightly slower inhalation, mouth slightly open, to prevent the fabric pulling against the lips. Under exertion he transitions to nose-only breathing to keep the seam from billowing — a tell that he is, despite outward composure, working.

### Head carriage

Level, slightly forward of true neutral by perhaps 5°, which puts the eye-line down a hair and forces interlocutors to feel addressed from above without his having to actually tilt his chin. Rotation is preferentially from the **cervical base** (a slow, full-neck turn) rather than from the eyes — he does not glance, he *regards.* When required to look quickly, the head precedes the eyes; the eyes do not dart independently. This is fencing eye-discipline, drilled out of childhood.

### The face beneath the hood (U)

The disfigurement is a topography of pulled and melted tissue across the lower two-thirds — the brow and orbital ridges relatively spared, the cheeks, lips, and jawline rendered into a smoothed, glassy distortion that does not move the way intact tissue moves. **Functional expressivity is concentrated in the eyes and the small zone of unbruised brow and temple.** This is why, masked, he is *more* readable than most men: every gram of expression he has access to is funnelled through the two openings, and a lifetime of practice has trained him to micro-modulate exactly there.

The eyes themselves: pale, set deep, with a fixed pupil discipline — he does **not** blink during the first thirty seconds of any interaction of consequence. Baseline blink rate at rest is approximately 8 per minute (low-normal trending toward suppressed); under threat it does not increase, it *decreases further*, which is the opposite of the normal sympathetic response and indicates trained inhibition.

### Grooming of the face he cannot show

Subject shaves daily, with a straight razor, despite the absence of any social need — large portions of the scarred surface no longer grow hair regularly. The shaving is done seated, in front of a mirror, with the cowl off, taking roughly 18 minutes — three times what is functionally required. This is **a sustained look at the wound he otherwise refuses to acknowledge**, performed in private ritual. He does not wince. He does not turn the head to favor an angle. The mirror is met dead-on.

The hair (where present, principally at the crown and occiput) is kept short, combed back, never product-glossy — a soldier's haircut on an aesthete's head. He cuts it himself rather than admit a barber to the unmasked face.

---

## IV. HANDS, GESTURE, AND THE ECONOMY OF MOVEMENT

The single most consistent observation across all surveillance eras: **he gestures less than he should.** A man of his erudition and verbal output would, statistically, produce 12–18 illustrative gestures per minute of speech; Helmut produces 2–4. The gestures he does deploy are *placements* rather than illustrations — the hand arrives at a position and stays there, marking a logical beat the way a conductor marks a downbeat.

**Catalogue of recurrent hand-gestures:**

- **The lifted index.** Right hand, palm down, index finger raised to about chin height, the other fingers softly curled. Marks a correction or a refinement of another speaker's point. Deployed roughly once per six-minute conversational segment with intellectual peers; almost never with subordinates (whom he does not correct, he *replaces*).
- **The open palm at the sternum.** Left hand, palm in, fingertips brushing the breastbone. Marks a personal commitment — *I will do this*, or *I have done this.* Rare. When it appears, the action it indexes is fixed and should be considered already executed.
- **The two-finger touch to the temple.** Right hand, index and middle finger laid against the right temple for a half-second. Appears when he is being asked a question whose answer he has known for a long time and is choosing whether to share. *Not* a thinking gesture; a *deciding* gesture.
- **The flat hand on the tabletop.** Already noted. Spread fingers, slight downward pressure. He is reading the room through the furniture.
- **The thumb-and-forefinger rub.** Almost never. When observed, it indicates he has identified, in real time, a flaw in his own plan. It is the closest thing he has to a tell, and only Moonstone and Songbird are known to have read it correctly in live conditions.

He does not point at people. He does not gesture above shoulder height. He does not strike the table. He does not wring his hands and has, to the camera's knowledge, never washed them with visible vigor.

The **sword-hand** — the right — is kept marginally more relaxed than the left during conversation. This is counterintuitive (the dominant hand should default to higher tone) and is the result of a deliberately maintained readiness: a relaxed hand draws faster than a tense one. Under threat, the relaxation deepens. He is most dangerous when his right hand looks asleep.

---

## V. SWORDWORK AS POSTURAL SIGNATURE

The sword at his side is not decoration; the body has *organized around it* since the age of seven. Observable consequences:

- **Asymmetric musculature.** Right forearm and posterior deltoid measurably heavier than left; right intercostal development; a slightly elevated right scapula at rest. Tailoring of his green tunic accommodates this — the right shoulder seam is set roughly 4mm higher than the left.
- **Hip-pocket pattern.** Subject does not place objects in the left hip area; the entire left flank is kept clear for the scabbard regardless of whether he is wearing one. This persists in civilian dress.
- **The half-second draw-check.** On entering any new space, the right hand drifts to where the sword-hilt would be, confirms presence or absence, and returns. Takes approximately 400 milliseconds and is performed unconsciously roughly six times per hour in unfamiliar environments.
- **En-garde collapse under threat.** When startled or threatened, the body does not enter a boxer's stance or a wrestler's crouch — it drops a quarter-inch into a fencer's preparation, rear knee bending first. This is so deeply grooved that it occurs even when he is unarmed and outnumbered, which has cost him at least one captivity escape.

He practices **solo drills** in cell or quarters daily: roughly 40 minutes of footwork (advance, retreat, lunge, balestra, fleche) and an additional 20 of empty-hand bladework using a folded towel, a chair leg, anything to hand. Cell-block surveillance from the Raft period shows this regimen interrupted only once, on the date of his father's death anniversary, when the drill collapsed into a static stance held for the full 60 minutes.

---

## VI. VOICE, BREATH, AND ORAL HABIT

**Vocal baseline.** Mid-baritone, German-substrate English with the **r** softened and the **w** kept slightly Germanic. Speaking rate is slow — approximately 110 words per minute against an educated-English median nearer 150. The slowness is not impediment; it is **information control.** Each syllable lands fully before the next is permitted to begin.

**Sentence shape.** Long syntactic units, subordinated, with a preference for the periodic sentence in which the verb arrives late. He does not interrupt. He does not finish others' sentences. He waits, sometimes for an uncomfortable count past the conversational beat, before responding — the silence is part of the dominance.

**Multilingual switching.** Native-fluent in German, English, French, Russian; functional in Italian, Latin, Sokovian dialect. He code-switches deliberately and *down* — speaking the interlocutor's weaker language to maintain margin. With a fellow polyglot he settles, by preference, into French, which he treats as the language of equals.

**Breath at rest.** Diaphragmatic, slow — 9 to 11 breaths per minute. Under exertion he transitions cleanly to a 2-in/4-out pattern that he can sustain through serious combat without audible respiratory distress. He does not gasp. He does not sigh. The **absence of the sigh** across thousands of recorded hours is itself a datum — sighing is an autonomic discharge of held tension, and he discharges that tension elsewhere (the daily fencing drill, the mirror-shave, the solo time with the unmasked face).

**Oral micro-habits.** Beneath the cowl, the tongue rests against the hard palate just behind the front teeth (suggested by speech production and the absence of the *th*-substrate dental drift his native German would predict). He does not chew his lip — the scar tissue would make it impossible to know if he were. He does not clear his throat habitually; when he does, it is once, quietly, and is deliberate punctuation.

**Laughter.** Rare and three-shaped: (1) a single dry exhalation through the nose, used dismissively, perhaps twenty times a day; (2) a short, real laugh — three syllables, descending — used perhaps once a month, almost always in response to a precise piece of wit from a true peer; (3) a soundless laugh visible only in the shoulders and the eye-creases, deployed when something has confirmed his estimation of human folly. He has never been recorded laughing out loud at his own joke.

---

## VII. EATING AND DRINKING

**Eating posture.** Continental hold (fork in left, knife in right, both retained throughout the meal). Cuts one bite ahead — never the American-style pre-cut. Bite size small and consistent. Chews 18–22 times before swallow; this is metronomic and does not vary with food type. He does not speak with food in his mouth and will permit a silence rather than rush a swallow.

**Pacing.** Slow. A standard meal takes him 45–60 minutes. He finishes the plate or he doesn't; partial plates are returned without comment. Food preferences trend toward Middle European — game, root vegetables, dark bread, strong cheese — and away from anything requiring the fingers. He does not eat finger food in company. In private he will eat an apple, peeled in a single unbroken spiral with a paring knife — the spiral is so consistent across surveillance instances that it should be treated as a *signature.*

**Drinking.** Wine with the meal — one glass, sipped, never finished within fifteen minutes of pour. Brandy after, in a snifter held by the bowl (warmed by the hand) rather than the stem. He swirls precisely three times before nosing. He does not toast first; he waits to be toasted to. He does not get drunk in any surveillance record. The **upper bound of his consumption** appears to be the point at which a second glass would be required, and he has *never been observed crossing it.*

**Water.** Drunk between courses, not during. Glass held by the rim, not the body — he does not warm his water.

**Unmasked eating.** Done alone. The cowl is removed for meals in private quarters; in the field it is lifted only enough to admit the rim of a cup, and food is deferred until cover is achieved. He will go 36 hours without solid food rather than unmask in mixed company.

---

## VIII. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Schedule.** Approximately 5.5 hours per night, split: roughly four hours from 23:30 to 03:30, then a 90-minute second sleep from approximately 05:00 to 06:30. The 03:30–05:00 interval is wakeful reading, correspondence, or sword-drill. This biphasic pattern is consistent across operational tempo and captivity, and is one of the most stable indicators in the file — *find Helmut Zemo awake between 0330 and 0500 and you have found him at his sharpest.*

**Position.** Supine, hands folded on the lower sternum, ankles uncrossed. He sleeps on the **back** despite the cervical strain a man of his age should expect; the position keeps the cowl, when worn (he sleeps masked in non-secure environments), from binding. Pillow used as cervical support, not head cushion — a small bolster, not the standard Western pillow.

**REM and movement.** Surveillance of captivity sleep shows minimal limb movement; sleep efficiency calculated at 91%+, which is exceptional for a man in his demographic and condition. Sleep talking: extremely rare and almost exclusively in German, single words, of which "Vater" and "nein" recur. No documented night terrors. Wakes without alarm at the intended hour ±3 minutes.

**The dream he is having** is, by definition, not in the file. The data the file *does* hold is the somatic shape of his return to consciousness: eyes open, body still for a count of three, then a single deep breath and a sit-up from the supine with no use of the hands — a sit-up he could not perform if his core were not held in the constant low engagement noted in section I.

---

## IX. SEXUALITY AND INTIMATE SOMATICS

The record is thin and the thinness is itself the datum. Across fifty years of observable life, the subject has formed no public attachment, sustained no documented partnership, and produced no heir. Liaisons that can be inferred are uniformly **brief, transactional, and conducted on his terms in his space.** He does not, as far as the file knows, kiss in public. He does not touch the small of a woman's back to guide her through a doorway. He does not place a possessive hand.

What the file *can* characterize:

- **Proxemics.** His personal space is unusually large for a European of his class — roughly 1.1 meters at the front, somewhat tighter at the flanks. He does not breach others' space casually and reads breach as either subordination (acceptable from inferiors who need correcting) or challenge.
- **Touch.** He initiates touch rarely and asymmetrically: a hand at the elbow to redirect; a single finger at the chin to compel eye contact (used with subordinates, never peers); a hand laid flat between the shoulder blades as either reassurance or sentence. He receives touch with a stillness that reads as permission rather than welcome.
- **The body as instrument, not vessel.** He treats his physicality as a sword treats its edge — maintained, sharpened, kept from rust, deployed for purpose. The erotic register, where it exists at all, appears subordinated to *mastery* (of an outcome, a person, a moment) rather than pleasure. The closest the file has come to an intimate destabilization in him is the Rogers-fixation, which has the structural features of an obsessional love and which he conducts with greater attention than any partner has received.

This is not asexuality; it is **the erotic capacity rationed almost entirely out of the budget** in service of the master project. A different man with the same body would have lived a different life. He chose this one.

---

## X. STATE-DEPENDENT SHIFTS — THE GRAMMAR OF CHANGE

The atlas above is the **baseline**. The diagnostic value of somatic surveillance is in the deltas. The following table reads the body across four states.

### A. Calm / strategic-mode (the operating baseline)

All of the above. The breath is slow, the hand on the table is flat-spread, the cowl is unfussed, the voice is measured. He is most lethal in this state and least visibly so. **Tell:** the periodic two-finger temple touch as he decides what to share. **False tell to discount:** the slight smile-shape in the corners of the eye-openings, which is voluntary and means whatever he wants it to mean.

### B. Stress (operational complication, plan deviation, unexpected variable)

The body **slows further** rather than speeding up. Blink rate drops from 8 to 4 per minute. The flat hand on the table presses harder — the knuckles whiten through the back of the glove. Speech rate decreases by another 10–15%, words become more periodic, syntactic units lengthen. The **thumb-forefinger rub** appears, sometimes only once, sometimes repeating. He stands rather than sits; the fencer's quarter-inch drop comes into the knees. He becomes courteous to a degree that should be considered an active warning sign — a Helmut Zemo who is using the formal *Sie* with a subordinate who has just failed him is preparing to dispose of that subordinate.

### C. Threat (Rogers in the room, Bucky-cue activated, Zemo name impugned)

This is the **failure state** and the file's most operationally important section. The previously iron postural discipline cracks in characteristic, predictable ways:

- The right hand abandons relaxation and *grips* — at the hilt if armed, at the air if not.
- Head carriage tilts forward another 3–5°; the chin drops; the eyes harden into a fixed sighting plane.
- Breathing accelerates and shallows — the only state in which his diaphragmatic discipline reliably fails.
- The mask is touched. **He touches the mask under high-Rogers-stress.** Not adjusts — *touches*, fingertips to the seam at the brow or the throat, as if confirming the wound is still covered. This is the most reliable destabilization indicator in the file and is invisible to anyone not looking for it.
- Speech rate *accelerates* — uniquely in this state, the slowness breaks. He talks more in Rogers's presence than he does in any other context. The polished syntax can degrade into something more vehement, more German, more openly aristocratic.
- The strategic-IQ collapse documented in the analytic workup has a somatic shape: the body **commits to a symbolic act** (the gloating, the spectacle, the gesture) and the eyes close for a fractional second at the moment of commitment, as if savoring. The closure of the eyes is the moment after which he will lose.

### D. Intimacy (the rare, narrow band)

He does not have intimacy with persons. He has intimacy with **objects and rituals**: the sword (handled with a tenderness reserved for nothing living), the mirror at shaving, the apple peeled in one spiral, the second-sleep wakefulness with a book, the anniversary stance held in silence. In these moments — observable only through deep surveillance and only briefly — the postural discipline relaxes into something closer to its true rest-state. The shoulders lower a finger's width *without* the conscious public version of the gesture. The breath deepens to 7–8 per minute. The mouth, beneath the cowl or above the unmasked ruin, can be seen to soften.

He is, in these moments, almost peaceful. They last between thirty seconds and four minutes. They end without warning, the discipline reasserting in a single inhalation, and he resumes the man he has built.

---

## XI. AGING DELTAS (LONGITUDINAL)

Across the surveillance window, the body has changed less than the chronology would predict — the régime he maintains is rigorous and the longevity exposures noted in the Medical section have, demonstrably or by inference, slowed the curve. Notable


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS
## UATU Dossier — Subject: Helmut Julius Fritz Zemo
### Section 4 of the Behavioral Synthesis

---

## 4.1 Attachment Style — Classification and Confidence

**Primary classification: Dismissive-Avoidant (Bartholomew Type 3), with a single arrested idealization at the core and a secondary disorganized fragment activated exclusively by Captain America.**

Confidence: high on the dismissive-avoidant designation, derived from fifty years of behavioral evidence across more than a dozen lead writers; high on the arrested-idealization overlay (Heinrich); high on the disorganized fragment (the Rogers cluster shows approach-avoid oscillation, intrusive cognition, and intimacy-coded hostility that does not fit a clean avoidant template).

The subject is **not** fearful-avoidant (he does not want closeness and fear it; he does not want it). He is **not** preoccupied (he does not seek reassurance or proximity). He is **not** secure (he has never demonstrated the capacity for a regulated, mutual, durable attachment of any kind). The dismissive-avoidant designation is the only one that accounts for the constellation: low expressed need for others, high self-reliance narrative, deactivation of attachment cues under stress, contempt for displays of dependency in others, and — the cleanest diagnostic — **the absence of loneliness as a depictable internal state.** Across thousands of pages of canon, no panel, no caption, no internal monologue shows him missing anyone. Even the father is not missed; the father is *avenged*, which is a different and characteristically narcissistic substitution.

---

## 4.2 Origins — The Developmental Ecology

Reconstructed from the few stable canonical pillars and the conspicuous silences around them.

**The father (Heinrich).** Present as figure, absent as person. By the time Helmut is old enough to form episodic memory, Heinrich is either in hiding in South America, conducting research at remove, or already dead. The father is therefore experienced not as a relational object but as a **mythological one** — letters, portraits, retainers' stories, the title itself. A child cannot form a real attachment to a myth; he can only worship it. Worship is a *defense* against attachment, not a form of it. This is the structural foundation.

**The mother (Hilda Zemo).** Canon's silence is the data point. Across half a century and dozens of writers handling deep backstory, no scene of her with the infant or child Helmut has been depicted; no recollection by him names her with feeling; no portrait of her is shown in any of his interiors. The dismissive-avoidant subject does not narrate the missing primary caregiver. He organizes a life around not requiring one and, in time, around not noticing the requirement was ever there. Whether Hilda was cold, dead early, ill, absented by the father's flight, or simply emotionally unavailable, the *outcome* is identifiable from behavior: no internalized maternal object. He cannot be soothed and does not expect to be.

**The household.** Retainers, tutors, fencing masters, librarians. A child raised by staff in a residence organized around a feud is socialized into hierarchy rather than reciprocity. Affection is delivered as service; service is delivered against payment of loyalty; loyalty is owed upward to the name. He learns very early that **the unit of relation is the contract, not the bond.** This is the operational code that governs every subsequent attachment he forms.

**The named enemy.** Captain America is installed in his cognitive architecture before he can read — a face on a wall, a story repeated, the man who killed Father. Long before he meets Rogers, Helmut has rehearsed Rogers's destruction in fantasy thousands of times. The relationship therefore *predates* their encounter, which means by the time it is consummated in combat it has the density of decades of one-sided intimacy. This is why the Rogers connection sits where attachment normally sits in the architecture of a self. **He grew up with no caregiver and one enemy, and the enemy got the slot.**

---

## 4.3 The Anatomy of How He Bonds (and Why It Is Not Really Bonding)

Helmut does not bond. He **contracts, recruits, and curates.** The taxonomy below describes the functional categories he uses in place of attachment.

**The Instrument.** Most subordinates. Selected for capability, retained for performance, discarded for failure. He is unfailingly courteous to instruments — the courtesy is a management technology, not warmth — and he remembers their names, capabilities, and operational quirks with eidetic precision. He will not avenge an instrument he loses. He may, however, replace one with deliberate care, because the *role* matters.

**The Asset.** A subset of instruments with rare or unique capabilities (Moonstone, the Fixer/Techno, Goliath, the Beetle iteration; in modernized terms, anyone whose value cannot be substituted). Assets receive more latitude, more information, more performative respect. He flatters them with the precise content their narcissism requires — Moonstone receives recognition of her intelligence; muscle receives recognition of their menace. He is, in this register, an excellent operational psychologist.

**The Peer.** Rare. Reserved for the handful he privately concedes might be his equal in some dimension — Karla Sofen (intellect plus manipulation), occasionally Osborn (ambition), the better generation of his V-Battalion antagonists. With peers he is warier, drier, less performative, and more dangerous. He does not enjoy peers. He notes them.

**The Adversary-Worthy.** A category of one for most of his life: Rogers. Expanded transiently to include Barnes-as-Winter-Soldier and a small number of others. The Adversary-Worthy receives the resources, attention, and continuity of cognition that a securely attached man would direct toward a spouse.

**The Audience.** The public, the press, the institutions he sometimes performs for. He understands the audience as a single composite mind with predictable hungers and feeds it accordingly. The Citizen V/Thunderbolts long con is the masterclass: he reads an exhausted, grieving public correctly down to the *register* of reassurance they require and supplies it for months without ever needing the supply reciprocated.

**Conspicuously absent categories:** Friend. Confidant. Lover-as-person (rather than lover-as-instrument). Mentor (he will train but he will not mentor; the relational density is missing). Child (he has, across all canon, never fathered nor expressed an interest in doing so — the lineage drive is *backward* facing, toward the redemption of ancestors, not *forward* toward descendants; this is itself diagnostic).

---

## 4.4 Distrust — The Default State and How It Operates

Helmut's baseline is not paranoia (which is reality-distorting) but **calibrated distrust** (which is reality-tracking). He assumes:

- Every subordinate would replace him if able.
- Every peer is running a parallel agenda.
- Every public alliance has a half-life measured in the duration of the shared enemy.
- Every confession is a probe.
- Every kindness is a transaction in deferred billing.

This baseline is held *without affect.* He is not anxious about it; he is organized around it. The cognitive load most people pay to maintain trust, he pays to maintain accounting. His ledgers are precise. He remembers every favor extended to him and every slight, and he carries forward both balances against the day they will be settled.
